Archetype Exemplar Decklists
============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 21, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











You've seen the [Top 8 decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpcop15/top-8-decklists-2015-06-21) and the [Top 16 decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/events/coverage/gpcop15/top-16-decklists-2015-06-21). But now it's time to delve a little deeper and feature the best-performing list of any archetype that did not make it to the Top 8 or Top 16.







#### Ian Farnung's Abzan Midrange – 18th place at Grand Prix Copenhagen 2015


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-eb68983be8716ae542a7e39ceda07e07.txt?n=Ian%20Farnung%27s%20Abzan%20Midrange%20%E2%80%93%2018th%20place%20at%20Grand%20Prix%20Copenhagen%202015)
